# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`

# Task: Implement Custom Header Injection Filter for Envoy

## Objective
Create a new HTTP filter `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection` that injects
configurable headers into requests and/or responses based on route metadata.

## Requirements

1. **Create filter source files**:
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h` — filter class declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc` — filter implementation
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h` — factory declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc` — factory registration

2. **Filter behavior**:
   - Implements `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` (request path) and `Http::StreamEncoderFilter` (response path)
   - Reads header injection rules from filter config
   - Supports both request and response header injection
   - Follows Envoy's filter lifecycle (decodeHeaders, encodeHeaders)

3. **Create test file**:
   - `test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter_test.cc`

## Key Reference Files
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.h` — simple header filter pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.cc` — implementation pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/config.cc` — factory registration
- `source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h` — factory base class

## Success Criteria
- Filter header file declares class inheriting from StreamDecoderFilter/StreamEncoderFilter
- Filter implementation has decodeHeaders/encodeHeaders methods
- Factory config file registers the filter
- Follows Envoy naming: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection
- Test file exists

## Summary of Implementation

### ✅ **Source Files Created**

1. **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h`**
   - Filter class declaration inheriting from `Http::StreamFilter`
   - Implements both `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` and `Http::StreamEncoderFilter`
   - Declares `decodeHeaders()` and `encodeHeaders()` methods
   - Config and callback storage

2. **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc`**
   - Filter implementation with request/response header injection logic
   - `decodeHeaders()` - injects headers into HTTP requests
   - `encodeHeaders()` - injects headers into HTTP responses
   - Configuration parsing and callback management

3. **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h`**
   - Factory class declaration extending `Common::FactoryBase`
   - Registers filter as `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection`

4. **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc`**
   - Factory implementation for creating filter instances
   - Supports both global and per-route configurations
   - Registers factory with Envoy's filter registry

5. **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/BUILD`**
   - Bazel build configuration for the filter

### ✅ **Protocol Buffer Definition**

6. **`api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.proto`**
   - `HeaderValue` message with `name` and `value` fields
   - `Config` message with `request_headers` and `response_headers` repeated fields
   - Proper package and options for code generation

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter {

/**
 * Configuration for the custom header injection filter.
 */
class Config : public ::Envoy::Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig,
               public Logger::Loggable<Logger::Id::config> {
public:
  Config(const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config config);

  struct HeaderInjection {
    std::string header_name;
    std::string header_value;
  };

  const std::vector<HeaderInjection>& requestHeaders() const { return request_headers_; }
  const std::vector<HeaderInjection>& responseHeaders() const { return response_headers_; }

private:
  std::vector<HeaderInjection> request_headers_;
  std::vector<HeaderInjection> response_headers_;
};

using ConfigSharedPtr = std::shared_ptr<Config>;

/**
 * Custom Header Injection filter that injects configurable headers into
 * requests and/or responses.
 */

2. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"

#include "source/common/http/utility.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter {

Config::Config(const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config config) {
  for (const auto& header : config.request_headers()) {
    request_headers_.push_back({header.name(), header.value()});
  }
  for (const auto& header : config.response_headers()) {
    response_headers_.push_back({header.name(), header.value()});
  }
}

CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(const ConfigSharedPtr config)
    : config_(config) {}

CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::~CustomHeaderInjectionFilter() = default;

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(
    Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool) {
  const auto* config = getConfig();

  for (const auto& header : config->requestHeaders()) {
    headers.setCopy(Http::LowerCaseString(header.header_name), header.header_value);
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

void CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::setDecoderFilterCallbacks(
    Http::StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks& callbacks) {
  decoder_callbacks_ = &callbacks;
}

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::encodeHeaders(
    Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool) {
  const auto* config = getConfig();

  for (const auto& header : config->responseHeaders()) {
    headers.setCopy(Http::LowerCaseString(header.header_name), header.header_value);
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

    Http::StreamEncoderFilter

4. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h"

#include <string>

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"
#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.validate.h"
#include "envoy/registry/registry.h"

#include "source/common/protobuf/utility.h"
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter {

Http::FilterFactoryCb CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config& proto_config,
    const std::string&, Server::Configuration::FactoryContext& context) {
  ConfigSharedPtr filter_config(std::make_shared<Config>(proto_config));

  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {
    callbacks.addStreamFilter(
        Http::StreamFilterSharedPtr{new CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(filter_config)});
  };
}

absl::StatusOr<Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfigConstSharedPtr>
CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config& config,
    Server::Configuration::ServerFactoryContext& context, ProtobufMessage::ValidationVisitor&) {
  return std::make_shared<const Config>(config);
}

/**
 * Static registration for the custom-header-injection filter.
 */
REGISTER_FACTORY(CustomHeaderInjectionConfig, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory);

} // namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy

5. WRITE /workspace/api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.proto
syntax = "proto3";

package envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3;

import "udpa/annotations/status.proto";
import "udpa/annotations/versioning.proto";
import "validate/validate.proto";

option java_package = "io.envoyproxy.envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3";
option java_outer_classname = "CustomHeaderInjectionProto";
option java_multiple_files = true;
option go_package = "github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3;custom_header_injectionv3";
option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = ACTIVE;

// [#protodoc-title: Custom Header Injection Filter]
//
// The configuration for injecting custom headers into requests and responses.
// [#extension: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection]

message HeaderValue {
  // The header name.
  string name = 1 [(validate.rules).string = {min_len: 1}];

  // The header value.
  string value = 2;
}

message Config {
  // Headers to inject into requests.
  repeated HeaderValue request_headers = 1;

  // Headers to inject into responses.
  repeated HeaderValue response_headers = 2;
}

6. WRITE /workspace/test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter_test.cc
#include <memory>

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"

#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

#include "test/mocks/http/mocks.h"
#include "test/test_common/utility.h"

#include "gmock/gmock.h"
#include "gtest/gtest.h"

using testing::_;
using testing::NiceMock;
using testing::Return;

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter {
namespace {

class CustomHeaderInjectionTest : public testing::Test {
public:
  const std::string request_config_yaml = R"EOF(
request_headers:
  - name: x-injected-request
    value: request-value
response_headers:
  - name: x-injected-response
    value: response-value
)EOF";

  void initializeFilter(const std::string& yaml) {
    envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config config;
    TestUtility::loadFromYaml(yaml, config);
    config_ = std::make_shared<Config>(config);
    filter_ = std::make_shared<CustomHeaderInjectionFilter>(config_);
    filter_->setDecoderFilterCallbacks(decoder_callbacks_);
    filter_->setEncoderFilterCallbacks(encoder_callbacks_);
  }

  ConfigSharedPtr config_;
  std::shared_ptr<CustomHeaderInjectionFilter> filter_;
  NiceMock<Http::MockStreamDecoderFilterCallbacks> decoder_callbacks_;
  NiceMock<Http::MockStreamEncoderFilterCallbacks> encoder_callbacks_;
};

/**
 * Test request header injection.
 */
TEST_F(CustomHeaderInjectionTest, InjectRequestHeaders) {
  initializeFilter(request_config_yaml);
  Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl headers;

  auto status = filter_->decodeHeaders(headers, false);

  EXPECT_EQ(status, Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue);
  EXPECT_EQ(headers.get("x-injected-request"), "request-value");
}
